# Current employment

1. TOC
{:toc}

Questions in the sections:

* Please select your organization type: one choice
* Which university do you work for?: one choice
* What is your official job title?: free text
* Are you known in your group by a different job title? If so, please enter the job title you use: free text
* Do you work full time or part time: free text
* What is the nature of your current employment?: one choice
* When did you start your current position?: numeric
* What is the expected duration (in years) of your current position (in total)?: numeric
* Please select the range of your salary: one choice
* Which of the following sources are used to pay for your effort as an RSE?: one choice


## Australia

### Type of organization

| Organisation type for Australia   |   Count |   Percentage |
|:----------------------------------|--------:|-------------:|
| University                        |      19 |       59.375 |
| Non-profit organization           |       4 |       12.5   |
| Government                        |       4 |       12.5   |
| Other                             |       2 |        6.25  |
| National laboratory               |       2 |        6.25  |
| NGO                               |       1 |        3.125 |

[Download CSV](/international-survey-2021/csv/organisation-type_australia.csv){: .button}

### In which field are you working

| in which field for Australia               |   Count |   Percentage |
|:-------------------------------------------|--------:|-------------:|
| Information and computing sciences         |      12 |       37.5   |
| Biomedical and clinical sciences           |       7 |       21.875 |
| Biological sciences                        |       6 |       18.75  |
| Earth sciences                             |       6 |       18.75  |
| Physical sciences                          |       6 |       18.75  |
| Health sciences                            |       6 |       18.75  |
| Language, communication and culture        |       5 |       15.625 |
| Built environment and design               |       5 |       15.625 |
| Engineering                                |       5 |       15.625 |
| Human society                              |       4 |       12.5   |
| Chemical sciences                          |       4 |       12.5   |
| Environmental sciences                     |       4 |       12.5   |
| History, heritage and archaeology          |       4 |       12.5   |
| Commerce, management, tourism and services |       4 |       12.5   |
| Education.1                                |       3 |        9.375 |
| Economics.1                                |       3 |        9.375 |
| Indigenous studies                         |       2 |        6.25  |
| Mathematical sciences                      |       2 |        6.25  |
| Psychology.1                               |       2 |        6.25  |
| Law and legal studies                      |       1 |        3.125 |
| Philosophy and religious studies           |       1 |        3.125 |
| Creative arts and writing                  |       1 |        3.125 |

### Length of current position

| Duration of contract in year for Australia (without 95 percentile)   |   Results in 2022 |   Results in 2018 |
|:---------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------:|------------------:|
| count                                                                |          19       |          74       |
| mean                                                                 |           2.94737 |           6.35473 |
| std                                                                  |           2.02    |           7.26787 |
| min                                                                  |           0       |           0.5     |
| 25%                                                                  |           1       |           2       |
| 50%                                                                  |           3       |           3       |
| 75%                                                                  |           4.25    |           6       |
| max                                                                  |           6       |          30       |

| Salary for Australia            |   Count |   Percentage |
|:--------------------------------|--------:|-------------:|
| &lt; AUD 45,000                    |       1 |      3.22581 |
| ≥ AUD 45,000 and &lt; AUD 65,000   |     nan |    nan       |
| ≥ AUD 65,000 and &lt; AUD 85,000   |       2 |      6.45161 |
| ≥ AUD 85,000 and &lt; AUD 105,000  |       7 |     22.5806  |
| ≥ AUD 105,000 and &lt; AUD 120,000 |      13 |     41.9355  |
| ≥ AUD 120,000                   |       8 |     25.8065  |

### Salary

| Salary for Germany             |   Count |   Percentage |
|:-------------------------------|--------:|-------------:|
| Less than 27.499 EUR           |       8 |     3.92157  |
| Between 27.500 and 32.999 EUR  |       5 |     2.45098  |
| Between 33.000 and 38.499 EUR  |      12 |     5.88235  |
| Between 38.500 and 43.999 EUR  |      12 |     5.88235  |
| Between 44.000 and 49.999 EUR  |      11 |     5.39216  |
| Between 50.000 and 54.999 EUR  |      37 |    18.1373   |
| Between 55.000 and 65.999 EUR  |      60 |    29.4118   |
| Between 66.000 and 76.999 EUR  |      36 |    17.6471   |
| Between 77.000 and 109.999 EUR |      15 |     7.35294  |
| More than 110.000 EUR          |       1 |     0.490196 |
| Prefer not to say              |       7 |     3.43137  |

### Length of current position

| Duration of contract in year for Netherlands (without 95 percentile)   |   Results in 2022 |   Results in 2018 |
|:-----------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------:|------------------:|
| count                                                                  |          21       |          38       |
| mean                                                                   |           2.5381  |           8.88158 |
| std                                                                    |           1.19184 |          11.4723  |
| min                                                                    |           1       |           1       |
| 25%                                                                    |           2       |           2       |
| 50%                                                                    |           2       |           4       |
| 75%                                                                    |           4       |           7       |
| max                                                                    |           4       |          50       |

### Salary

| Salary for Netherlands         |   Count |   Percentage |
|:-------------------------------|--------:|-------------:|
| Less than 27.499 EUR           |       2 |      3.50877 |
| Between 27.500 and 32.999 EUR  |       2 |      3.50877 |
| Between 33.000 and 38.499 EUR  |       6 |     10.5263  |
| Between 38.500 and 43.999 EUR  |       4 |      7.01754 |
| Between 44.000 and 49.999 EUR  |       7 |     12.2807  |
| Between 50.000 and 54.999 EUR  |      10 |     17.5439  |
| Between 55.000 and 65.999 EUR  |      10 |     17.5439  |
| Between 66.000 and 76.999 EUR  |       4 |      7.01754 |
| Between 77.000 and 109.999 EUR |       4 |      7.01754 |
| More than 110.000 EUR          |       1 |      1.75439 |
| Prefer not to say              |       7 |     12.2807  |

### Funding

| Type of funding for Netherlands                                                                        |   Count |   Percentage |
|:-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--------:|-------------:|
| Institutional support                                                                                  |      32 |     48.4848  |
| Grants                                                                                                 |      24 |     36.3636  |
| Industry support                                                                                       |       6 |      9.09091 |
| Foundations &amp; consortiums                                                                              |       5 |      7.57576 |
| Consulting &amp; services                                                                                  |       2 |      3.0303  |
| Venture capital                                                                                        |       1 |      1.51515 |
| other. Which of the following sources are used to pay for your effort as a Research Software Engineer? |       1 |      1.51515 |

| Duration of contract in year for New Zealand (without 95 percentile)   |   Results in 2022 |   Results in 2018 |
|:-----------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------:|------------------:|
| count                                                                  |           4       |            25     |
| mean                                                                   |           2.5     |            11.872 |
| std                                                                    |           1.29099 |            13.362 |
| min                                                                    |           1       |             0     |
| 25%                                                                    |           1.75    |             2     |
| 50%                                                                    |           2.5     |            10     |
| 75%                                                                    |           3.25    |            12     |
| max                                                                    |           4       |            45     |

### Salary

| Salary for New Zealand          |   Count |   Percentage |
|:--------------------------------|--------:|-------------:|
| &lt; NZD 45,000                    |     nan |     nan      |
| ≥ NZD 45,000 and &lt; NZD 65,000   |       3 |      11.5385 |
| ≥ NZD 65,000 and &lt; NZD 85,000   |       6 |      23.0769 |
| ≥ NZD 85,000 and &lt; NZD 105,000  |       7 |      26.9231 |
| ≥ NZD 105,000 and &lt; NZD 120,000 |       3 |      11.5385 |
| ≥ NZD 120,000                   |       5 |      19.2308 |

### Funding

| Type of funding for New Zealand                                                                        |   Count |   Percentage |
|:-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--------:|-------------:|
| Institutional support                                                                                  |      15 |     53.5714  |
| Grants                                                                                                 |      10 |     35.7143  |
| Consulting &amp; services                                                                                  |       5 |     17.8571  |
| Industry support                                                                                       |       4 |     14.2857  |
| other. Which of the following sources are used to pay for your effort as a Research Software Engineer? |       1 |      3.57143 |
| SaaS                                                                                                   |       1 |      3.57143 |

| 25%                                                                       |           2       |           2.375   |

### Salary

| Salary for United Kingdom   |   Count |   Percentage |
|:----------------------------|--------:|-------------:|
| &lt; £18,031                   |       4 |     2.72109  |
| ≥ £18,031 and &lt; £24,057     |       1 |     0.680272 |
| ≥ £24,057 and &lt; £32,277     |       9 |     6.12245  |
| ≥ £32,277 and &lt; £43,325     |      64 |    43.5374   |
| ≥ £43,325 and &lt; £58,172     |      40 |    27.2109   |
| ≥ £58,172                   |      21 |    14.2857   |

### Length of current position

| Duration of contract in year for United States (without 95 percentile)   |   Results in 2022 |   Results in 2018 |
|:-------------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------:|------------------:|
| count                                                                    |          21       |         100       |
| mean                                                                     |           2.97619 |           8.458   |
| std                                                                      |           1.83355 |           8.13265 |
| min                                                                      |          -1       |           0.8     |
| 25%                                                                      |           2       |           3       |
| 50%                                                                      |           2       |           5       |
| 75%                                                                      |           5       |          10       |
| max                                                                      |           6       |          37       |

### Funding

| Type of funding for United States                                                                      |   Count |   Percentage |
|:-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--------:|-------------:|
| Institutional support                                                                                  |      85 |       53.125 |
| Grants                                                                                                 |      82 |       51.25  |
| Foundations &amp; consortiums                                                                              |      11 |        6.875 |
| Industry support                                                                                       |       9 |        5.625 |
| Consulting &amp; services                                                                                  |       9 |        5.625 |
| other. Which of the following sources are used to pay for your effort as a Research Software Engineer? |       8 |        5     |
| Donation button                                                                                        |       2 |        1.25  |
| SaaS                                                                                                   |       1 |        0.625 |
| Open core                                                                                              |       1 |        0.625 |
| Crowdfunding (recurring)                                                                               |       1 |        0.625 |
| Advertising &amp; sponsorships                                                                             |       1 |        0.625 |

### Length of current position

| Duration of contract in year for World (without 95 percentile)   |   Results in 2022 |   Results in 2018 |
|:-----------------------------------------------------------------|------------------:|------------------:|
| count                                                            |          87       |           39      |
| mean                                                             |           2.82414 |            9      |
| std                                                              |           1.35397 |           10.2444 |
| min                                                              |           0       |            1      |
| 25%                                                              |           2       |            2      |
| 50%                                                              |           3       |            4      |
| 75%                                                              |           4       |           13.5    |
| max                                                              |           6       |           35      |
